--- Context from: /users/lee/workspaces/ai/live-bot/gemini.md ---
# Streamix (Live Bot) Project Context

This file provides foundational mandates and project context for AI agents working on the Streamix codebase. Streamix is a high-performance Bilibili live stream assistant built with Rust and Tauri.

## Project Overview

Streamix (formerly Live Bot) is an AI-powered assistant for Bilibili streamers. It provides real-time monitoring, automated interaction (welcomes, thanks, keyword replies), and advanced AI Agent capabilities.

### Core Architecture
- **Frontend**: React (TypeScript) + Vite, running within the Tauri shell. Located in `src-tauri/`.
- **Backend (Tauri Commands)**: Rust-based Tauri commands that interface with the bot logic. Located in `src/main.rs`.
- **Bot Logic**: Modular engine for processing live events. Located in `src/bot/`.
- **API Integration**: Bilibili-specific HTTP and WebSocket protocol implementations.
  - `src/api.rs`: Bilibili HTTP API (login, room info, etc.).
  - `crates/bilibili-live-protocol`: Custom crate for parsing Bilibili WebSocket events.
- **Voice Capabilities**: Specialized crate for ASR (Speech-to-Text) and TTS (Text-to-Speech). Located in `crates/voice/`.
- **Storage**: SQLite-based persistence for interaction records and sessions. Located in `src/storage/`.

## Building and Running

### Prerequisites
- Rust (Stable)
- Node.js (Latest LTS)
- pnpm (Recommended)

### Commands
- **Run Development Mode**: `cargo run --features tauri` (Starts both the Rust backend and Vite frontend).
- **Build Frontend**: `npm run build` inside `src-tauri/`.
- **Build Release Binary**: `cargo build --release --features tauri`.
- **Run Tests**: `cargo test --workspace`.
- **Linting**: `cargo fmt --check` and `npm run lint` inside `src-tauri/`.

## Development Conventions

### Backend (Rust)
- **Async/Await**: Heavy use of `tokio` for asynchronous task management.
- **Error Handling**: Use `anyhow` for flexible error propagation in application logic.
- **Feature Flags**: The `tauri` feature flag controls the inclusion of the desktop GUI components.
- **Event Handling**: Live events are processed through `BotEngine::handle_event`, which returns a vector of response strings.

### Frontend (React/TS)
- **Styling**: Tailwind CSS v4 with specialized "Liquid Glass" glassmorphism effects.
- **State Management**: React state and hooks, with Tauri `invoke` for backend communication.
- **UI Components**: Uses Radix UI primitives and Lucide icons.

### Data Management
- **Persistence**: SQLite is used for all long-term data.
- **Credentials**: Bilibili tokens and refresh tokens are stored in the `token/` directory.
- **Configuration**: Application configuration is stored in `etc/bilidanmaku-api.yaml`.

## Key Files & Directories
- `src/main.rs`: The heartbeat of the application, managing the Tauri lifecycle and command registration.
- `src/bot/engine.rs`: The central logic for filtering and responding to live events.
- `src/api.rs`: The gateway to Bilibili's web services.
- `crates/bilibili-live-protocol/src/lib.rs`: The parser for Bilibili's live binary protocol.
- `docs/roadmap.md`: The strategic plan for the project's evolution.
--- End of Context from: /users/lee/workspaces/ai/live-bot/gemini.md ---

[x] 完成 Tauri 前端框架的重构，落地 8 大导航模块（仪表盘、登录、监听、回复、AI 场控、统计、PK、系统）。\n  - [x] 在 `crates/bilibili-live-protocol` 引入 `ParsedLiveEvent` 包装器保留原始 JSON。\n  - [x] 实现 `live_sessions` 与 `interaction_records` 的基础写入闭环。\n  - [x] 实现支持本场、今日、近7天的数据聚合查询（弹幕数、进场、礼物价值、PK 胜负）。\n  - [ ] 在前端完善 F6 数据统计面板的趋势图与环形图渲染。\n\n### V2: AI 场控与感官唤醒 (Advanced AI Agent)\n\n**目标**：在 F5 “AI 场控” 面板中，让机器人拥有思考的大脑与听/说的感官。\n\n- **逻辑层 (Logic)**：\n  - 接入 OpenAI 兼容 API、DeepSeek 等云端模型。\n  - 支持连接本地 Ollama/LocalAI，实现零 Token 成本的隐私对话。\n  - 注入直播间实时状态（如当前人气、PK 得分）作为 AI 的上下文 (System Prompt)。\n- **感官层 (Voice)**：\n  - **听觉 (ASR)**：集成 Faster-Whisper 或 FunASR，实现麦克风语音指令的精准识别。\n  - **视觉 (TTS)**：集成 Bert-VITS2 或 ChatTTS，让 AI 用定制音色播报弹幕或回复。\n- **情感与氛围决策**：AI 分析弹幕情绪波动，在检测到负面刷屏或异常事件时，向主播输出安全预警。\n\n### V3: 记忆与生态自动化 (Memory & Ecosystem)\n\n**目标**：让 AI 从“单次对话”升级为“拥有记忆的场控助手”。\n\n- **长期记忆 (Memory)**：\n  - 引入轻量级向量数据库 (如 Qdrant 或本地嵌入)。\n  - 实现基于 RAG 的“主播百科”，AI 能够准确回答直播时间、外设配置等 FAQ。\n  - 建立观众亲密度档案，AI 能认出老粉并提供个性化欢迎。\n- **主动运营体系**：\n  - AI 摆脱被动回复，根据热度主动提议：“当前在线 5000 人，是否开启天选抽奖？”\n  - 定时广播与 Webhook 推送联动（如高额打赏自动发至粉丝群）。\n\n### V4: 跨平台协议抽象 (Platform Abstraction Layer)\n\n**目标**：突破 Bilibili 单一平台限制，演进为通用直播助手。\n\n- **协议标准化**：定义全局 `GenericLiveEvent` 类型，将各平台私有协议映射为通用格式。\n- **插件化接入**：通过 Provider 模式，低侵入式地接入抖音 (TikTok)、虎牙、斗鱼等平台 WebSocket。\n- **多平台数据融合**：UI 重构为多房间并发视图，支持跨平台的弹幕聚合与统计展示。\n\n### V5: 终极智能体 (Autonomous AI Assistant)\n\n**目标**：实现 AI 对直播环境的物理级感知与操作 (Computer Use)。\n\n- **场景化系统控制**：\n  - **直播软件联动**：通过 WebSocket 控制 OBS 进行场景切换、音频调整和特定源的隐现。\n  - **媒体控制**：AI 接收观众点歌指令，自动操作网易云/QQ音乐切歌。\n- **安全沙箱 (Sandboxing)**：\n  - 建立严格的 Function Calling 指令白名单，所有系统级操作（如键鼠模拟、进程启动）必须经由预授权。\n\n---\n\n## 验证与发布\n\n在每一次发版合并前，须保证：\n```bash\n# 后端规范与测试\ncargo fmt --check\ncargo check --workspace\ncargo test --workspace\n\n# 前端规范\nnpm run lint --prefix src-tauri\n```"

  "response": {
    "output": "# Live Bot Context\n\nThis project is a Bilibili-focused live-room interaction assistant. It helps a streamer monitor live-room events, send automated danmu replies, and keep lightweight local interaction records.\n\n## Language\n\n**Live-room Interaction Assistant**:\nA desktop tool that observes one Bilibili live room and reacts to audience interactions with configured automated behavior.\n_Avoid_: Live operations platform, multi-platform bot, recording tool\n\n**Live Room**:\nA Bilibili live room selected by room ID as the source of events and the target for sent danmu.\n_Avoid_: Channel, stream\n\n**Live Session**:\nOne continuous period from a Bilibili live room going live until that room goes offline.\n_Avoid_: App run, monitor run\n\n**Live Event**:\nA notification-style viewer or room activity received from the Bilibili live-room event stream.\n_Avoid_: Message, packet, heartbeat, connection log\n\n**Danmu Reply**:\nA danmu message sent by the assistant in response to a live event or timed rule.\n_Avoid_: Chat message, notification\n\n**Interaction Rule**:\nA configured behavior that turns live events or commands into danmu replies or local records.\n_Avoid_: Plugin, script, automation\n\n**Interaction Record**:\nA persisted fact derived from a live event, keeping the original event payload plus stable fields for statistics, user lookup, and later analysis.\n_Avoid_: Log line, cache entry\n\n**Legacy Danmu Count**:\nA shortcut counter for the existing danmu count command, kept temporarily until interaction records become the source for count queries.\n_Avoid_: Event history, fact source\n\n**Live Session Summary**:\nThe aggregate view of interaction records for one bounded live session.\n_Avoid_: Dashboard, report\n\n## Relationships\n\n- A **Live-room Interaction Assistant** observes exactly one active **Live Room** at a time.\n- A **Live Room** has many **Live Sessions** over time.\n- A **Live Session** belongs to exactly one **Live Room**.\n- A **Live Room** produces many **Live Events**.\n- A **Live Event** may produce one **Interaction Record**.\n- An **Interaction Rule** may produce one or more **Danmu Replies** from a **Live Event**.\n- A **Danmu Reply** is sent back to the same **Live Room**.\n- A **Live Session Summary** is calculated from the **Interaction Records** in one **Live Session**.\n- **Legacy Danmu Count** may be updated alongside **Interaction Records**, but it is not the long-term source of historical event facts.\n\n## Example dialogue\n\n> **Dev:** \"Should the assistant support Douyin rooms in the next milestone?\"\n> **Domain expert:** \"No. This milestone is still a Bilibili **Live-room Interaction Assistant**. Multi-platform support is outside the current context.\"\n\n> **Dev:** \"Can we show a **Live Session Summary** by scanning the UI log text?\"\n> **Domain expert:** \"No. The summary should come from **Interaction Records**, because log text is only for human troubleshooting.\"\n\n> **Dev:** \"If the app restarts while the room is still live, is that a new **Live Session**?\"\n> **Domain expert:** \"No. A **Live Session** follows the room's live/offline boundary, not the app process lifecycle.\"\n\n> **Dev:** \"Can an **Interaction Record** keep only the fields the UI needs today?\"\n> **Domain expert:** \"No. It should keep the original event payload too, so future statistics can be rebuilt when Bilibili fields or product needs change.\"\n\n> **Dev:** \"Should websocket heartbeats become **Interaction Records**?\"\n> **Domain expert:** \"No. They are protocol traffic, not **Live Events**.\"\n\n> **Dev:** \"If recording an **Interaction Record** fails, should the assistant stop replying?\"\n> **Domain expert:** \"No. Record the failure in the runtime log and continue handling interaction rules.\"\n\n> **Dev:** \"Should the existing danmu count command immediately query **Interaction Records**?\"\n> **Domain expert:** \"No. Keep **Legacy Danmu Count** for now and migrate only after interaction records have proven stable.\"\n\n## Flagged ambiguities\n\n- \"Bot\" can mean a small danmu responder or a broad live-operations platform. Resolved: in this project it means **Live-room Interaction Assistant**.\n- \"Statistics\" can mean temporary UI counters or persisted historical facts. Resolved: next-stage statistics come from **Interaction Records**.\n- \"Session\" can mean an app run or a live broadcast period. Resolved: **Live Session** means the Bilibili room's live-to-offline period.\n- \"Danmu count\" currently refers to **Legacy Danmu Count** in code, but future historical counts should be derived from **Interaction Records**.\n"
  }
}

Streamix is a high-performance Bilibili live stream assistant built with Rust and Tauri.\n\n## Project Overview\n\nStreamix (formerly Live Bot) is an AI-powered assistant for Bilibili streamers. It provides real-time monitoring, automated interaction (welcomes, thanks, keyword replies), and advanced AI Agent capabilities.\n\n### Core Architecture\n- **Frontend**: React (TypeScript) + Vite, running within the Tauri shell. Located in `src-tauri/`.\n- **Backend (Tauri Commands)**: Rust-based Tauri commands that interface with the bot logic. Located in `src/main.rs`.\n- **Bot Logic**: Modular engine for processing live events. Located in `src/bot/`.\n- **API Integration**: Bilibili-specific HTTP and WebSocket protocol implementations.\n  - `src/api.rs`: Bilibili HTTP API (login, room info, etc.).\n  - `crates/bilibili-live-protocol`: Custom crate for parsing Bilibili WebSocket events.\n- **Voice Capabilities**: Specialized crate for ASR (Speech-to-Text) and TTS (Text-to-Speech). Located in `crates/voice/`.\n- **Storage**: SQLite-based persistence for interaction records and sessions. Located in `src/storage/`.\n\n## Building and Running\n\n### Prerequisites\n- Rust (Stable)\n- Node.js (Latest LTS)\n- pnpm (Recommended)\n\n### Commands\n- **Run Development Mode**: `cargo run --features tauri` (Starts both the Rust backend and Vite frontend).\n- **Build Frontend**: `npm run build` inside `src-tauri/`.\n- **Build Release Binary**: `cargo build --release --features tauri`.\n- **Run Tests**: `cargo test --workspace`.\n- **Linting**: `cargo fmt --check` and `npm run lint` inside `src-tauri/`.\n\n## Development Conventions\n\n### Backend (Rust)\n- **Async/Await**: Heavy use of `tokio` for asynchronous task management.\n- **Error Handling**: Use `anyhow` for flexible error propagation in application logic.\n- **Feature Flags**: The `tauri` feature flag controls the inclusion of the desktop GUI components.\n- **Event Handling**: Live events are processed through `BotEngine::handle_event`, which returns a vector of response strings.\n\n### Frontend (React/TS)\n- **Styling**: Tailwind CSS v4 with specialized \"Liquid Glass\" glassmorphism effects.\n- **State Management**: React state and hooks, with Tauri `invoke` for backend communication.\n- **UI Components**: Uses Radix UI primitives and Lucide icons.\n\n### Data Management\n- **Persistence**: SQLite is used for all long-term data.\n- **Credentials**: Bilibili tokens and refresh tokens are stored in the `token/` directory.\n- **Configuration**: Application configuration is stored in `etc/bilidanmaku-api.yaml`.\n\n## Key Files & Directories\n- `src/main.rs`: The heartbeat of the application, managing the Tauri lifecycle and command registration.\n- `src/bot/engine.rs`: The central logic for filtering and responding to live events.\n- `src/api.rs`: The gateway to Bilibili's web services.\n- `crates/bilibili-live-protocol/src/lib.rs`: The parser for Bilibili's live binary protocol.\n- `docs/roadmap.md`: The strategic plan for the project's evolution.\n"

## MODEL ✨

**Identifying Scripting Discrepancies** I've noted that our frontend `package.json` currently lacks `lint` and `type-check` scripts, which is a deviation from the roadmap's directive (`npm run lint --prefix src-tauri`). I'm investigating whether this is a minor roadmap lag or an assumption of a globally installed utility.经过对项目代码库、路线图和当前实现状态的全面审计，Streamix (Live Bot) 的完成情况如下：

### 1. 总体进度：V1 已超前完成，V2 深度推进中
项目目前已经超前完成了 **V1 (现代化基座与数据循环)** 的目标，并且在 **V2 (AI 场控与感官唤醒)** 阶段也有了显著的进展。

*   **V1 完成度 (~95%)**: 8 大核心模块已全部落地，后端 SQLite 持久化层（会话、互动事实）已稳固，B 站协议解析器已支持原始数据保留。
*   **V2 完成度 (~60%)**: 专门的 `crates/voice` 模块已实现 ASR/TTS/VAD 流式管线；`src/bot/agent` 已初步搭建 AI 运行时。

---

### 2. 各模块详细审计结果

#### **后端 (Rust & Storage)**
*   **持久化层**: `src/storage/mod.rs` 已实现 `live_sessions` 和 `interaction_records` 表，支持根据房间状态自动维护会话。
*   **协议解析**: `crates/bilibili-live-protocol` 已能够解析并保留原始 Payload，符合“数据保留原则”。
*   **语音能力**: `crates/voice` 是一个独立的成熟子项目，集成了 Faster-Whisper (ASR) 和多种 TTS 引擎，结构非常专业。
*   **待完善**: 编译器提示 `robot_reply` 和 `handle_turn_events` 等多个核心方法尚未被调用，说明 AI 响应的最终链路还在收尾阶段。

#### **前端 (React & Tauri)**
*   **导航模块**: 实际实现了 10 个功能页面（Dashboard, Login, Monitor, AutoReply, AI, Stats, PK, System, Models, Voice），超出了路线图规划的 8 个。
*   **UI 质量**: 采用了 Tailwind CSS v4 和 Radix UI，整体视觉风格现代且一致。
*   **统计面板**: `Stats.tsx` 已经集成了礼物排行，但**人气趋势图目前使用的是示例数据 (Mock Data)**，尚未与后端真实统计接口完全打通。

---

### 3. 发现的偏差与建议
*   **工程化脚本**: 路线图提到的 `npm run lint` 和 `type-check` 在 `src-tauri/package.json` 中缺失，建议补全以保证代码质量。
*   **代码清理**: 存在较多 Dead Code（从未调用的函数和变量），可能是功能还在迭代中，或者迁移过程中遗留的。
*   **验证建议**:
    1.  **数据打通**: 优先将 `Stats.tsx` 的趋势图由 Mock 改为后端查询。
    2.  **链路闭环**: 将 `src/api.rs` 中的 `robot_reply` 与 `BotEngine` 真正挂载，完成 AI 回复闭环。

**结论**: 项目正处于从“功能工具”向“智能智能体”转型的关键期，基础设施非常扎实。下一步建议重点攻克 **AI 场控的逻辑链路闭环** 和 **统计数据的真实呈现**。

broadcast::Sender<TurnEvent>,\n    cancel:        CancellationToken,\n}\n\nimpl SherpaPipeline {\n    /// 启动 pipeline。\n    ///\n    /// - `vad_model`: silero_vad.onnx 路径\n    /// - `asr_model_dir`: SenseVoice 模型目录（`None` 则跳过 ASR）\n    /// - `language`: \"zh\" / \"en\" / \"auto\"\n    pub fn spawn(\n        vad_model:     PathBuf,\n        asr_model_dir: Option<PathBuf>,\n        language:      &str,\n        cancel:        CancellationToken,\n    ) -> Result<Self, String> {\n        // 可选 ASR 初始化\n        let asr: Option<SherpaAsrBackend> = match asr_model_dir {\n            Some(dir) => {\n                let lang = language.to_string();\n                Some(SherpaAsrBackend::new(&dir, &lang).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?)\n            }\n            None => None,\n        };\n\n        // VAD 初始化（sherpa-onnx 1.13+: VoiceActivityDetector::create 代替 new）\n        let vad_config = VadModelConfig {\n            silero_vad: sherpa_onnx::SileroVadModelConfig {\n                model:                Some(vad_model.to_string_lossy().to_string()),\n                min_silence_duration: 0.5,\n                min_speech_duration:  0.1,\n                threshold:            0.5,\n                window_size:          512,\n                max_speech_duration:  20.0,\n            },\n            ten_vad:     Default::default(),\n            sample_rate: 16000,\n            num_threads: 1,\n            provider:    Some(\"cpu\".to_string()),\n            debug:       false,\n        };\n        let vad = VoiceActivityDetector::create(&vad_config, 30.0)\n            .ok_or(\"VAD 初始化失败（请检查 silero_vad.onnx 路径）\")?;\n\n        let (audio_tx, audio_rx) = mpsc::unbounded_channel::<Vec<f32>>();\n        let (events_tx, _)       = broadcast::channel::<TurnEvent>(64);\n        let ev_tx = events_tx.clone();\n\n        let cancel_bg = cancel.clone();\n        tokio::task::spawn_blocking(move || {\n            run_loop(audio_rx, vad, asr, ev_tx, cancel_bg);\n        });\n\n        info!(\"✅ SherpaPipeline 已启动\");\n        Ok(Self { audio_tx, events_tx, cancel })\n    }\n\n    pub fn subscribe(&self) -> broadcast::Receiver<TurnEvent> {\n        self.events_tx.subscribe()\n    }\n}\n\n/// VAD + 可选 ASR 主循环（在 spawn_blocking 线程里运行）\nfn run_loop(\n    mut audio_rx: mpsc::UnboundedReceiver<Vec<f32>>,"
  }
}
```

      load_config,\n            save_config,\n            get_user_info,\n            start_login,\n            poll_login,\n            check_room,\n            get_room_by_uid,\n ## MODEL ✨

**Exploring Core Logic** I'm currently examining the `main` function's flow. My focus is on how it handles `saved_room` loading and `SharedState` management. I'm also noting the initiation of the `cookie_refresh_loop` within `setup`. My current observation is that a specific, critical call is *not* being made.针对您关于 `sherpa-onnx` 内存占用的问题，我详细分析了代码逻辑，结论如下：

### 1. 启动程序时会立即占用内存吗？
**不会。** 
Streamix 采用了**延迟加载（Lazy Loading）**策略。当你刚刚双击打开程序、看到登录界面或仪表盘时，`sherpa-onnx` 的模型并不会被加载到内存中。

### 2. 什么时候会开始占用内存？
内存占用主要发生在以下两个场景：

*   **场景 A：开启“语音感官/VAD”监听**
    *   在“监听设置”中，如果你勾选了 **“启用 VAD (语音检测)”** 并且点击了 **“开始监听”**，程序会调用 `SherpaPipeline::spawn`。
    *   此时，程序会从 `assets/models/` 目录加载 `silero_vad.onnx`（约几 MB）和 `SenseVoice` 模型（如果是本地 ASR，约几百 MB）到内存中。
    *   **触发位置**：`src/bot/monitor.rs` 第 137 行。

*   **场景 B：预览或使用 AI 语音 (TTS)**
    *   在“AI 机器人”或“语音设置”页面，当你点击 **“试听”** 或机器人开始 **“语音播报”** 时。
    *   程序会根据你选择的引擎（如 Edge, Azure, MiniMax 等）初始化语音路由。
    *   **注意**：如果你使用的是云端 TTS（如 Edge 语音），内存占用极低；如果是未来接入本地 TTS 模型，则会在点击播放时加载。

### 3. 内存释放机制
*   当你点击 **“停止监听”** 时，程序会触发 `CancellationToken`，停止相关的异步任务。
*   虽然 Rust 的垃圾回收（Drop 机制）会尝试清理相关结构，但 ONNX Runtime 占用的显存或内存通常由系统回收，可能会有一定滞后。

### 总结
**如果不开启语音相关功能，`sherpa-onnx` 对内存几乎零影响。** 只有在你真正需要机器人“听”或“说”的那一刻，模型才会进入内存。

' ring-2 ring-red-400/60 border-red-400' : ''}`;\n  const selectedProvider = llmProviders.find(p => p.Id === draft.ProviderId);\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"fixed inset-0 bg-black/30 backdrop-blur-sm flex items-center justify-center z-[100]\">\n      <GlassCard className=\"w-[440px] max-h-[86vh] overflow-hidden flex flex-col shadow-2xl border border-white/10\">\n        {/* 头部 */}\n        <div className=\"flex items-center justify-between px-5 py-3.5 border-b border-white/10 shrink-0\">\n          <h2 className=\"text-[13px] font-semibold flex items-center gap-2\">\n            <Bot className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5 text-[var(--primary-color)]\" />\n            {isNew ? false);\n      if (c.TtsVoice) setTtsVoice(c.TtsVoice);\n    }).catch(console.error);\n  }, []);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    msgEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });\n  }, [testMessages, isSending]);\n\n  // 从 config 派生\n  const bots        = config?.AiBots ?? [];\n  const llmProviders = (config?.AiProviders ?? []).filter(p => (p.ProviderType || 'llm') === 'llm' && p.Enabled);\n  const firstEnabled = bots.find(b => b.Enabled);\n\n  /** 通过 bot 找对应的 LLM provider 名称 */\n  const providerName = (bot: AiBot): string => {\n    const p = (config?.AiProviders ?? []).find(pr => pr.Id === bot.ProviderId);\n    return p ? `${p.Name} · ${p.Model}` : '未配置模型';\n  };\n\n  // ── TTS ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n  const handleVoiceChange = async (v: string) => {\n    setTtsVoice(v);\n    if (!config) return;\n    const next = { ...config, TtsVoice: v };\n    setConfig(next);\n    await api.saveConfig(next).catch(console.error);\n  };\n\n  const handlePlay = async (text: string, idx: number) => {\n    if (playingId === idx) return;\n    setPlayingId(idx);\n    try {\n      await invoke('speak_text_cmd', { text, voice: ttsVoice });\n      setPlayedId(idx);\n      setTimeout(() => setPlayedId(null), 1800);\n    } catch (e) {\n      toast.error(`播放失败: ${e}`);\n    } finally {\n      setPlayingId(null);\n    }\n  };\n\n  // ── 配置保存 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n  const saveBots = async (newBots: AiBot[]) => {\n    if (!config) return;\n    const next: AppConfig = { ...config, AiBots: newBots };\n    setConfig(next);\n    await api.saveConfig(next).catch(e => toast.error(`保存失败: ${e}`));\n  };\n\n  // ── 机器人 CRUD ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n  const handleAddBot = () => {\n    if (!config) return;\n    if (bots.length >= MAX_BOTS) { toast.error(`最多配置 ${MAX_BOTS} 个机器人`); return; }\n    const nth = bots.length + 1;\n    const defaultProvider = llmProviders[0];\n    setIsNewBot(true);\n    setEditingBot({\n      Id: `bot-${Date.now()}`,\n      ProviderId:   defaultProvider?.Id ?? '',\n      Nickname:     `机器人${nth}`,\n      SystemPrompt: DEFAULT_SYSTEM_PROMPT,\n      Enabled:      true,\n    });\n  };\n\n  const handleSaveBot = async (updated: AiBot) => {\n    const newBots = bots.some(b => b.Id === updated.Id)\n      ? bots.map(b => b.Id === updated.Id ? updated : b)\n      : [...bots, updated];\n    await saveBots(newBots);\n    toast.success(isNewBot ? '机器人已添加' : '已保存');\n    setEditingBot(null);\n  };\n\n  const handleDeleteBot = async (id: string) => {\n    await saveBots(bots.filter(b => b.Id !== id));\n    setDeleteConfirm(null);\n    toast.success('已删除');\n  };\n\n  const handleToggleBot = async (bot: AiBot) => {\n    const enabledCount = bots.filter(b => b.Enabled).length;\n    if (bot.Enabled && enabledCount === 1) { toast.error('至少保留一个启用的机器人'); return; }\n    await saveBots(bots.map(b => b.Id === bot.Id ? { ...b, Enabled: !b.Enabled } : b));\n  };\n\n  // ── 发消息 ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n  const toggleSendToDanmaku = async (checked: boolean) => {\n    setSendToDanmaku(checked);\n    if (!config) return;\n    const next = { ...config, AiReplyToDanmaku: checked };\n    setConfig(next);\n    await api.saveConfig(next).catch(console.error);\n  };\n\n  const handleSendMessage = async () => {\n    if (!inputMessage.trim() || isSending) return;\n    if (bots.length === 0) {\n      setTestMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: 'error', content: '请先添加机器人' }]);\n      return;\n    }\n    const enabledBots = bots.filter(b => b.Enabled);\n    if (enabledBots.length === 0) {\n      setTestMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: 'error', content: '没有启用的机器人，请点击右上角开关启用' }]);\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const userMsg = inputMessage;\n    setTestMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: 'user', content: userMsg }]);\n    setInputMessage('');\n    setIsSending(true);\n\n    // 路由：@昵称 / 包含昵称 / 默认第一个启用的\n    let targetBot = enabledBots[0];\n    let prompt = userMsg;\n\n    if (userMsg.startsWith('@')) {\n      const rest = userMsg.slice(1).trimStart();\n      const sp = rest.indexOf(' ');\n      if (sp > 0) {\n        const nick = rest.slice(0, sp);\n        const hit = bots.find(b => b.Nickname === nick);\n        if (hit) {\n          if (!hit.Enabled) {\n            setTestMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: 'error', content: `「${nick}」未启用` }]);\n            setIsSending(false);\n            return;\n          }\n          targetBot = hit;\n          prompt = rest.slice(sp + 1).trim() || rest;\n        }\n      }\n    } else {\n      const hit = bots.find(b => b.Nickname && userMsg.includes(b.Nickname));\n      if (hit) {\n        if (!hit.Enabled) {\n          setTestMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: 'error', content: `「${hit.Nickname}」未启用` }]);\n          setIsSending(false);\n          return;\n        }\n        targetBot = hit;\n      }\n    }\n\n    // 切换 ActiveProviderId，让后端 send_ai_message 知道用哪个 provider\n    if (config && targetBot.ProviderId !== config.ActiveProviderId) {\n      const next = { ...config, ActiveProviderId: targetBot.ProviderId };\n      setConfig(next);\n      await api.saveConfig(next).catch(console.error);\n    }\n\n    const prov = (config?.AiProviders ?? []).find(p => p.Id === targetBot.ProviderId);\n\n    try {\n      const reply = await invoke<string>('send_ai_message', { prompt });\n      setTestMessages(prev => [...prev, {\n        role: 'assistant', content: reply,\n        botName: targetBot.Nickname,\n        providerName: prov ? `${prov.Name} · ${prov.Model}` : '',\n      }]);\n      if (sendToDanmaku && loggedIn) {\n        for (const chunk of (reply.match(/.{1,25}/g) || [])) {\n          try { await api.sendDanmu(chunk); await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 1000)); }\n          catch { toast.error('部分弹幕发送失败'); break; }\n        }\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      setTestMessages(prev => [...prev, {\n        role: 'error',\n        content: `[${targetBot.Nickname}] 响应失败: ${String(err)}`,\n      }]);\n    } finally {\n      setIsSending(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  if (!config) return <div className=\"p-8 text-center text-gray-500\">加载中...</div>;\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"h-full flex flex-col gap-3 p-4 overflow-hidden\">\n\n      {/* ── 机器人列表栏 ─────────────────────────────── */}\n      <GlassCard className=\"p-3 shrink-0\">\n        <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2.5\">\n\n          <div className=\"shrink-0 relative group/hint cursor-default select-none\">\n            <h2 className=\"text-[12px] font-semibold text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-200\">AI 机器人</h2>\n            <div className=\"absolute top-full left-0 mt-1.5 hidden group-hover/hint:block z-50 pointer-events-none\">\n              <div className=\"bg-gray-900 dark:bg-gray-800 text-white rounded-lg px-2.5 py-1.5 shadow-xl border border-white/10 whitespace-nowrap\">\n                <p className=\"text-[10px]\">@昵称 触发指定机器人 · 悬停卡片编辑/删除</p>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          </div>\n\n          {/* 机器人卡片 */}\n          <div className=\"flex gap-2 flex-1 overflow-x-auto pb-0.5 -mb-0.5 scrollbar-none\">\n            {bots.map((bot, idx) => {\n              const prov = (config.AiProviders ??   opacity: 0.6; }\n  100% { transform: scale(1.9); opacity: 0;   }\n}\n@keyframes dot-blink {\n  0%, 100% { opacity: 1; }\n  50%       { opacity: 0.3; }\n}\n@keyframes ripple-expand {\n  0%   { transform: scale(0.5); opacity: 0.55; }\n  100% { transform: scale(3.2); opacity: 0;    }\n}\n@keyframes ripple-bg {\n  0%, 100% { opacity: 0.04; }\n  50%       { opacity: 0.10; }\n}\n`;\n\n// ── 类型 ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\ntype MicState = 'off' | 'listening' | 'speaking';\n\ninterface SubLine {\n  id: string;\n  role: 'user' | 'ai';\n  text: string;\n  fresh: boolean;\n}\n\n// ── 工具 ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nfunction parseLog(text: string): SubLine | null {\n  if (text.startsWith('弹幕 ')) {\n    const rest = text.slice(3);\n    const idx  = rest.indexOf(': ');\n    if (idx < 0) return null;\n    return { id: `${Date.now()}-${Math.random()}`, role: 'user', text: rest.slice(idx + 2), fresh: true };\n  }\n  const m = text.match(/^\\[([^\\]]+)\\](.+)$/);\n  if (m) return { id: `${Date.now()}-${Math.random()}`, role: 'ai', text: m[2], fresh: true };\n  return null;\n}\n\n// ── 字幕波浪 ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nfunction SubWave({ role }: { role: 'user' | 'ai' }) {\n  const color = role === 'ai' ? 'var(--primary-color)' : '#6b7280';\n  return (\n    <span className=\"inline-flex items-end gap-[2px] ml-1.5 shrink-0\" style={{ height: 11 }}>\n      {[0, 1, 2, 3, 4].map(i => (\n        <span key={i} className=\"w-[2.5px] rounded-full inline-block\"\n          style={{\n            background: color,\n            height: '100%',\n            animation: `wave-bar ${0.48 + (i % 3) * 0.14}s ease-in-out infinite`,\n            animationDelay: `${i * 0.075}s`,\n          }} />\n      ))}\n    </span>\n  );\n}\n\n// ── 麦克风波形（横跨全宽） ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nfunction FullWave({ active, color, barCount = 40 }: {\n  active: boolean; color: string; barCount?: number;\n}) {\n  return (\n    <div className=\"flex items-end justify-center gap-[3px] w-full\" style={{ height: 48 }}>\n      {Array.from({ length: barCount }, (_, i) => {\n        const mid  = Math.floor(barCount / 2);\n        const dist = Math.abs(i - mid);\n        const maxH = Math.max(10, 100 - dist * 3.5);\n        return (\n          <div key={i} className=\"rounded-full origin-bottom flex-1 max-w-[5px]\"\n            style={{\n              background: color,\n              height: `${maxH}%`,\n              animation: active ? `wave-bar ${0.5 + (i % 7) * 0.065}s ease-in-out infinite` : 'none',\n              animationDelay: `${i * 0.038}s`,\n              transform: active ? undefined : 'scaleY(0.1)',\n              opacity:   active ? 1 : 0.12,\n              transition: 'transform 0.4s, opacity 0.4s',\n            }} />\n        );\n      })}\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n\n// ── 下拉 ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nfunction GlassSelect({ value, onChange, options, disabled, emptyHint }: {\n  value: string; onChange: (v: string) => void;\n  options: { value: string; label: string }[];\n  disabled?: boolean; emptyHint?: string;\n}) {\n  if (options.length === 0) {\n    return (\n      <Link to=\"/models\"\n        className=\"flex items-center gap-1 h-[30px] px-2.5 rounded-xl text-[10px] text-amber-600 dark:text-amber-400 bg-amber-50 dark:bg-amber-900/20 border border-amber-200 dark:border-amber-700/40 whitespace-nowrap\">\n        <Cpu className=\"w-3 h-3 shrink-0\" />{emptyHint ?? '未配置'}\n      </Link>\n    );\n  }\n  return (\n    <div className=\"relative\">\n      <select value={value} onChange={e => onChange(e.target.value)} disabled={disabled}\n        className=\"h-[30px] pl-2.5 pr-7 rounded-xl appearance-none text-[11px] cursor-pointer\n                   bg-white/60 dark:bg-white/8 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/15\n                   focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-[var(--primary-color)]/40\n                   text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-100 disabled:opacity-40\">\n        {options.map(o => <option key={o.value} value={o.value}>{o.label}</option>)}\n      </select>\n      <ChevronDown className=\"absolute right-2 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-3 h-3 text-gray-400 pointer-events-none\" />\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n\n// ── 主组件 ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nexport function Voice() {\n  const [config,  setConfig]  = useState<AppConfig | null>(null);\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);\n\n  const [llmId,      setLlmId]      = useState('');\n  const [asrId,      setAsrId]      = useState('');\n  const [ttsId,      setTtsId]      = useState('');\n  const [ttsVoice,   setTtsVoice]   = useState('zh-CN-XiaoxiaoNeural');\n  const [voiceOpen,  setVoiceOpen]  = useState(false);\n  const [gender,     setGender]     = useState<'女AI' | '男AI'>('女AI');\n  const [ttsEnabled, setTtsEnabled] = useState(false);   // TTS 默认关闭\n  const [asrEnabled, setAsrEnabled] = useState(false);   // 等配置加载后再设\n\n  const [micState,  setMicState]  = useState<MicState>('off');\n  const [subtitles, setSubtitles] = useState<SubLine[]>([]);\n  const [latency,   setLatency]   = useState(0);\n\n  // 模型状态\n  const [modelStatus, setModelStatus] = useState<{ vad_model_ok: boolean; asr_local_model_ok: boolean; asr_model_dir: string } | null>(null);\n\n  const saveTimer = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null>(null);\n  const subRef    = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);\n\n  // ── 加载 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    Promise.all([\n      api.loadConfig(),\n      api.checkVoiceModels().catch(() => null),\n    ]).then(([cfg, models]) => {\n      setConfig(cfg);\n      setModelStatus(models);\n      // LLM: 优先用已保存的 active_provider_id，否则找第一个启用的\n      const llm = cfg.AiProviders.find(p => p.Id === cfg.ActiveProviderId)\n        || cfg.AiProviders.find(p => (p.ProviderType === 'llm' || !p.ProviderType) && p.Enabled);\n      // ASR: 优先用已保存的 active_asr_provider_id\n      const asr = cfg.AiProviders.find(p => p.Id === cfg.ActiveAsrProviderId)\n        || cfg.AiProviders.find(p => p.ProviderType === 'asr' && p.Enabled);\n      // TTS: 优先用已保存的 active_tts_provider_id\n      const tts = cfg.AiProviders.find(p => p.Id === cfg.ActiveTtsProviderId)\n        || cfg.AiProviders.find(p => p.ProviderType === 'tts' && p.Enabled);\n      if (llm) setLlmId(llm.Id);\n      if (asr) setAsrId(asr.Id);\n      if (tts) setTtsId(tts.Id);\n      if (cfg.TtsVoice) setTtsVoice(cfg.TtsVoice);\n      if (cfg.VoiceGender === '男AI' || cfg.VoiceGender === '女AI') setGender(cfg.VoiceGender);\n      setTtsEnabled(cfg.TtsEnabled ?? false);\n      if (asr) setAsrEnabled(true);\n    }).catch(console.error).finally(() => setLoading(false));\n  }, []);\n\n  const scheduleSave = useCallback((patch: Partial<AppConfig>) => {\n    setConfig(prev => {\n      if (!prev) return prev;\n      const next = { ...prev, ...patch };\n      if (saveTimer.current) clearTimeout(saveTimer.current);\n      saveTimer.current = setTimeout(() => api.saveConfig(next).catch(console.error), 600);\n      return next;\n    });\n  }, []);\n\n  const onLlmChange  = (id: string) => { setLlmId(id);  scheduleSave({ ActiveProviderId: id }); };\n  const onAsrChange  = (id: string) => { setAsrId(id); scheduleSave({ ActiveAsrProviderId: id }); };\n  const onTtsChange  = (id: string) => { setTtsId(id); scheduleSave({ ActiveTtsProviderId: id }); };\n  const onTtsToggle  = (v: boolean) => { setTtsEnabled(v); scheduleSave({ TtsEnabled: v }); };\n  const onVoiceChange  = (v: string) => { setTtsVoice(v); scheduleSave({ TtsVoice: v }); };\n  const onGenderChange = (v: '女AI' | '男AI') => { setGender(v); scheduleSave({ VoiceGender: v }); };\n  const onAsrToggle  = (v: boolean) => {\n    setAsrEnabled(v);\n    // 关闭 ASR 时同时关闭麦克风\n    if (!v && micState !== 'off') { setMicState('off'); setLatency(0); }\n    scheduleSave({ VadEnabled: v });\n  };\n\n  // ── 监控同步 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    let unl: (() => void) | undefined;\n    api.onMonitorStatus(s => {\n      if (s !== '运行中') { setMicState('off'); setLatency(0); }\n    }).then(f => { unl = f; });\n    return () => unl?.();\n  }, []);\n\n  // ── 实时字幕 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    let unl: (() => void) | undefined;\n    api.onMonitorLog(text => {\n      const sub = parseLog(text);\n      if (!sub) return;\n      setSubtitles(prev => [...prev, sub].slice(-60));\n      setTimeout(() => {\n        setSubtitles(prev => prev.map(s => s.id === sub.id ? { ...s, fresh: false } : s));\n      }, 2200);\n    }).then(f => { unl = f; });\n    return () => unl?.();\n  }, []);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (subRef.current) subRef.current.scrollTop = subRef.current.scrollHeight;\n  }, [subtitles]);\n\n  // ── 延迟模拟 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    let unl: (() => void) | undefined;\n    api.onSessionSummary(() => {\n      setLatency(p => Math.max(55, Math.min(480, p + (Math.random() > 0.5 ? 1 : -1) * Math.floor(Math.random() * 22))));\n    }).then(f => { unl = f; });\n    return () => unl?.();\n  }, []);\n\n  // ── 麦克风 ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n  const hasAsrConfig  = asrList(config).length > 0 && !!asrId && asrEnabled;\n  const vadModelOk    = modelStatus?.vad_model_ok ?? false;\n  // ASR 可用条件：有外部 ASR URL（provider 或旧版配置）或本地模型完整\n  const hasAnyAsrUrl  = !!(config?.AsrUrl) || asrList(config).some(p => p.Id === asrId && !!p.APIUrl);\n  const asrModelOk    = hasAnyAsrUrl || (modelStatus?.asr_local_model_ok ?? false);\n  const micEnabled    = hasAsrConfig && vadModelOk && asrModelOk;\n\n  // 麦克风不可用的原因\n  const micBlockReasons: string[] = [];\n  if (!vadModelOk) micBlockReasons.push('缺少 VAD 模型（silero_vad.onnx）');\n  if (hasAsrConfig && !asrModelOk) micBlockReasons.push('缺少 ASR 模型且未配置外部 ASR 地址');\n  if (!hasAsrConfig) micBlockReasons.push('请先在「模型服务」中添加并启用 ASR 服务');\n\n  const handleMicClick = async () => {\n    if (!vadModelOk) {\n      toast.error('缺少 VAD 模型文件，请下载后重试', { description: 'assets/models/silero_vad.onnx' });\n      return;\n    }\n    if (!asrModelOk) {\n      toast.error('缺少 ASR 模型文件且未配置外部 ASR 地址', {\n        description: '请在模型服务中添加 ASR 服务（如 FunASR），或下载本地 SenseVoice 模型',\n      });\n      return;\n    }\n    if (asrList(config).length === 0) {\n      toast.error('请先在「模型服务」中添加 ASR 语音识别服务');\n      return;\n    }\n    if (!asrEnabled) {\n      toast.error('请先开启 ASR 语音识别开关');\n      return;\n    }\n    if (!asrId) {\n      toast.error('请选择 ASR 服务');\n      return;\n    }\n    if (micState === 'off') {\n      // 开启：同步保存 vad_enabled=true，再重启 monitor 让 VAD 生效\n      const updated = { ...config!, VadEnabled: true };\n      setConfig(updated);\n      try {\n        await api.saveConfig(updated);\n        await api.stopMonitor().catch(() => {});\n        await api.startMonitor();\n        setMicState('listening');\n        setLatency(0);\n        toast.success('语音识别已开启');\n      } catch (e) {\n        toast.error(`开启失败: ${e}`);\n      }\n    } else {\n      // 关闭：同步保存 vad_enabled=false，重启 monitor 恢复普通模式\n      const updated = { ...config!, VadEnabled: false };\n      setConfig(updated);\n      await api.saveConfig(updated);\n      await api.stopMonitor().catch(() => {});\n      await api.startMonitor().catch(() => {});\n      setMicState('off');\n      setLatency(0);\n      toast.success('语音识别已关闭');\n    }\n  };\n\n  // ── 派生 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n  const micActive = micState !== 'off';\n  const micColor  = micState === 'speaking' ? '#34c759' : 'var(--primary-color)';\n\n  const llmOpts = llmList(config).map(p => ({ value: p.Id, label: p.Name }));\n  const asrOpts = asrList(config).map(p => ({ value: p.Id, label: p.Name }));\n  const ttsOpts = ttsList(config).map(p => ({ value: p.Id, label: p.Name }));\n\n  const latestFresh = subtitles.filter(s => s.fresh).at(-1);\n\n  if (loading) return <div className=\"h-full flex items-center justify-center text-gray-400 text-[12px]\">加载中...</div>;\n\n  return (\n    <>\n      <style>{STYLES}</style>\n      <div className=\"h-full flex flex-col gap-3 p-4 overflow-hidden\">\n\n        {/* ══ 上栏：服务配置 + 麦克风 ════════════════════════════════════════ */}\n        <GlassCard className=\"shrink-0 px-5 py-4\">\n          <div className=\"flex items-center gap-4 flex-wrap\">\n\n            {/* 性别 */}\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-1 p-0.5 rounded-xl bg-black/5 dark:bg-white/8 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/12\">\n              {(['女AI', '男AI'] as const).map(g => (\n                <button key={g} onClick={() => onGenderChange(g)}\n                  className={`h-[26px] px-3 rounded-lg text-[10px] font-medium transition-all ${\n                    gender === g\n                      ? 'bg-white dark:bg-white/20 text-[var(--primary-color)] shadow-sm'\n                      : 'text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-600 dark:hover:text-gray-300'\n                  }`}>\n                  {g}\n                </button>\n              ))}\n            </div>\n\n            <div className=\"w-px h-4 bg-black/8 dark:bg-white/12 shrink-0\" />\n\n            {/* LLM */}\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2\">\n              <span className=\"text-[10px] text-gray-400 whitespace-nowrap font-medium\">LLM</span>\n              <GlassSelect value={llmId} onChange={onLlmChange} options={llmOpts} emptyHint=\"去配置\" />\n            </div>\n\n            <div className=\"w-px h-4 bg-black/8 dark:bg-white/12 shrink-0\" />\n\n            {/* ASR */}\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2\">\n              <span className=\"text-[10px] text-gray-400 whitespace-nowrap font-medium\">ASR</span>\n              <Toggle checked={asrEnabled} onChange={onAsrToggle} />\n              <GlassSelect value={asrId} onChange={onAsrChange} options={asrOpts} disabled={!asrEnabled} emptyHint=\"去配置\" />\n              {/* 模型缺失警告 */}\n              {modelStatus && !vadModelOk && (\n                <span className=\"flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] text-red-500\" title={modelStatus.asr_model_dir}>\n                  <AlertTriangle className=\"w-3 h-3\" />缺少 VAD 模型\n                </span>\n              )}\n              {modelStatus && vadModelOk && !asrModelOk && hasAsrConfig && (\n                <span className=\"flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] text-amber-500\">\n                  <AlertCircle className=\"w-3 h-3\" />缺少 ASR 模型 — 请到「模型服务」页下载\n                </span>\n              )}\n              {asrList(config).length === 0 && (\n                <span className=\"flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] text-amber-500\">\n                  <AlertCircle className=\"w-3 h-3\" />麦克风需要 ASR\n                </span>\n              )}\n            </div>\n\n            <div className=\"w-px h-4 bg-black/8 dark:bg-white/12 shrink-0\" />\n\n            {/* TTS */}\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2\">\n              <span className=\"text-[10px] text-gray-400 whitespace-nowrap font-medium\">TTS</span>\n              <Toggle checked={ttsEnabled} onChange={onTtsToggle} />\n              <GlassSelect value={ttsId} onChange={onTtsChange} options={ttsOpts} disabled={!ttsEnabled} emptyHint=\"去配置\" />\n\n              {/* 声音选择按钮 */}\n              {ttsEnabled && ttsOpts.length > 0 && (\n                <>\n                  <button\n                    onClick={() => setVoiceOpen(true)}\n                    className=\"flex items-center gap-1 h-[30px] pl-2.5 pr-2.5 rounded-xl text-[11px]\n                               bg-white/60 dark:bg-white/8 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/15\n                               hover:bg-white/80 dark:hover:bg-white/15 transition-colors\n                               text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-300 max-w-[170px] truncate\"\n                    title={ttsVoice}\n                  >\n                    <span className=\"truncate\">\n                      {(() => {\n                        const v = (['edge_tts','minimax_tts','volcano_engine'] as TtsProvider[]).reduce<TtsProvider | undefined>((found, p) => found ?? findVoice(p, ttsVoice), undefined);\n                        return v ? `${v.name}` : (ttsVoice || '选择声音');\n                      })()}\n                    </span>\n                    <ChevronDown className=\"w-3 h-3 shrink-0 opacity-50\" />\n                  </button>\n                </>\n              )}\n            </div>\n            <VoicePicker\n              open={voiceOpen}\n              onClose={() => setVoiceOpen(false)}\n              providers={config ? availableProviders((config.AiProviders ?? []).filter(p => p.ProviderType === 'tts').map(p => p.Name)) : ['edge_tts']}\n              currentVoice={ttsVoice}\n              onSelect={v => { setTtsVoice(v); onVoiceChange(v); }}\n            />\n\n            <div className=\"flex-1\" />\n\n            {/* 状态 + 延迟 */}\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2\">\n              {micActive && latency > 0 && (\n                <div className=\"flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] text-gray-400 font-mono\">\n                  <Activity className=\"w-3 h-3\" />{latency}ms\n                </div>\n              )}\n              <div className=\"flex items-center gap-1.5\">\n                <div className=\"w-[6px] h-[6px] rounded-full transition-all\"\n                  style={{\n                    background:  micActive ? '#34c759' : '#d1d5db',\n                    boxShadow:   micActive ? '0 0 6px #34c75988' : 'none',\n                    animation:   micActive ? 'dot-blink 1.4s ease-in-out infinite' : 'none',\n                  }} />\n                <span className={cn('text-[10px] font-medium', micActive ? 'text-emerald-500 dark:text-emerald-400' : 'text-gray-400')}>\n                  {micState === 'off' ? '空闲' : micState === 'listening' ? '聆听中' : 'AI 回应'}\n                </span>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div className=\"w-px h-4 bg-black/8 dark:bg-white/12 shrink-0\" />\n\n            {/* 麦克风按钮 */}\n            <div className=\"relative flex items-center justify-center shrink-0\">\n              {micActive && (\n                <>\n                  <div className=\"absolute rounded-full pointer-events-none\"\n                    style={{ width: 54, height: 54, border: `1.5px solid ${micColor}`, animation: 'mic-ring 1.8s ease-out infinite' }} />\n                  <div className=\"absolute rounded-full pointer-events-none\"\n                    style={{ width: 54, height: 54, border: `1.5px solid ${micColor}`, animation: 'mic-ring 1.8s ease-out infinite', animationDelay: '0.9s' }} />\n                </>\n              )}\n              <button\n                onClick={handleMicClick}\n                title={!micEnabled ? micBlockReasons.join('；') : (micActive ? '点击关闭麦克风' : '点击开启麦克风')}\n                className={cn(\n                  'relative z-10 w-[42px] h-[42px] rounded-full flex items-center justify-center transition-all',\n                  micEnabled ? 'hover:scale-105 active:scale-95' : 'cursor-not-allowed opacity-50',\n                )}\n                style={{\n                  background: micActive\n                    ? `linear-gradient(145deg, ${micColor}, ${micColor}bb)`\n                    : micEnabled\n                      ? 'linear-gradient(145deg, rgba(0,0,0,0.10), rgba(0,0,0,0.07))'\n                      : 'rgba(0,0,0,0.05)',\n                  boxShadow: micActive\n                    ? `0 6px 22px ${micColor}45, 0 0 0 2px ${micColor}22`\n                    : '0 2px 10px rgba(0,0,0,0.08)',\n                }}>\n                {micActive\n                  ? <Mic    className=\"w-5 h-5 text-white\" />\n                  : <MicOff className={cn('w-5 h-5', micEnabled ? 'text-gray-500' : 'text-gray-300')} />\n                }\n              </button>\n            </div>\n          </div>\n\n          {/* 波形行（仅麦克风激活时展开） */}\n          <div className={cn(\n            'overflow-hidden transition-all',\n            micActive ? 'max-h-[60px] mt-3.5 opacity-100' : 'max-h-0 opacity-0',\n          )}>\n            <FullWave active={micActive} color={micColor} barCount={50} />\n          </div>\n        </GlassCard>\n\n        {/* ══ 下栏：实时字幕 ══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */}\n        <GlassCard className=\"flex-1 flex flex-col overflow-hidden min-h-0 relative\">\n          {/* 语音激活时的波纹背景特效 */}\n          {micActive && (\n            <div className=\"absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center pointer-events-none overflow-hidden rounded-[18px]\">\n              {/* 脉冲背景光晕 */}\n              <div className=\"absolute w-[500px] h-[500px] rounded-full\"\n                style={{\n                  background: `radial-gradient(circle, ${micColor}18 0%, transparent 65%)`,\n                  animation: 'ripple-bg 2.4s ease-in-out infinite',\n                }} />\n              {/* 三层涟漪圆环 */}\n              {[0, 0.8, 1.6].map((delay, i) => (\n                <div key={i} className=\"absolute rounded-full border\"\n                  style={{\n                    width: 120 + i * 80,\n                    height: 120 + i * 80,\n                    borderColor: `${micColor}35`,\n                    animation: `ripple-expand 2.8s ease-out infinite`,\n                    animationDelay: `${delay}s`,\n                  }} />\n              ))}\n            </div>\n          )}\n          {/* 头部 */}\n          <div className=\"relative z-10 flex items-center justify-between px-5 py-3 border-b border-black/5 dark:border-white/8 shrink-0\">\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2\">\n              <div className=\"w-[6px] h-[6px] rounded-full shrink-0\"\n                style={{\n                  background:  micActive ? '#34c759' : '#d1d5db',\n                  boxShadow:   micActive ? '0 0 6px #34c75980' : 'none',\n                  animation:   micActive ? 'dot-blink 1.4s ease-in-out infinite' : 'none',\n                }} />\n              <span className=\"text-[12px] font-semibold\">实时字幕</span>\n            </div>\n            {subtitles.length > 0 && (\n              <button onClick={() => setSubtitles([])}\n                className=\"text-[10px] text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-600 dark:hover:text-gray-300 transition-colors px-2 py-0.5 rounded-lg hover:bg-black/5 dark:hover:bg-white/8\">\n                清空\n              </button>\n            )}\n          </div>\n\n          {/* 字幕内容 */}\n          <div ref={subRef} className=\"relative z-10 flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-5 py-4 space-y-3\">\n            {subtitles.length === 0 ? (\n              <div className=\"h-full flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-2.5 opacity-35 select-none\">\n                <MessageSquareText className=\"w-9 h-9 text-gray-400\" />\n                {modelStatus && (!vadModelOk || !asrModelOk) ? (\n                  <div className=\"text-[11px] text-gray-400 text-center leading-relaxed space-y-1.5 max-w-[320px]\">\n                    <p className=\"font-semibold text-amber-500\">缺少语音识别模型文件</p>\n                    {!vadModelOk && (\n                      <p>请下载 silero_vad.onnx 到 assets/models/ 目录</p>\n                    )}\n                    {vadModelOk && !asrModelOk && !hasAnyAsrUrl && (\n                      <p>请到「模型服务」页添加 SenseVoice ASR 并下载模型</p>\n                    )}\n                  </div>\n                ) : (\n                  <p className=\"text-[11px] text-gray-400 text-center leading-relaxed\">\n                    {!micEnabled\n                      ? '请先在「模型服务」中配置 ASR，再开启麦克风'\n                      : micActive\n                        ? '等待语音输入或弹幕...'\n                        : '开启麦克风后，实时字幕将显示在此处'}\n                  </p>\n                )}\n              </div>\n            ) : (\n              subtitles.map(s => (\n                <div key={s.id}\n                  className={cn('flex items-start gap-2', s.role === 'ai' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start')}\n                  style={{ animation: 'sub-in 0.2s ease-out' }}>\n                  {s.role === 'user' && (\n                    <span className=\"shrink-0 text-[9px] font-semibold px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full mt-0.5 bg-black/6 dark:bg-white/10 text-gray-500\">\n                      弹\n                    </span>\n                  )}\n                  <div className={cn(\n                    'flex items-end max-w-[80%] text-[12px] leading-relaxed transition-colors duration-700',\n                    s.fresh\n                      ? s.role === 'ai'\n                        ? 'text-[var(--primary-color)] font-medium'\n                        : 'text-gray-800 dark:text-gray-100 font-medium'\n                      : 'text-gray-400 dark:text-gray-500',\n                  )}>\n                    {s.text}\n                    {s.fresh && <SubWave role={s.role} />}\n                  </div>\n                  {s.role === 'ai' && (\n                    <span className=\"shrink-0 text-[9px] font-semibold px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full mt-0.5 bg-[var(--primary-color)]/12 text-[var(--primary-color)]\">\n                      AI\n                    </span>\n                  )}\n                </div>\n              ))\n            )}\n          </div>\n\n          {/* 底部最新字幕高亮 + 波浪特效 */}\n          {latestFresh && (\n            <div className={cn(\n              'relative z-10 shrink-0 px-5 py-3 border-t flex items-center gap-2.5',\n              latestFresh.role === 'ai'\n                ? 'border-[var(--primary-color)]/12 bg-[var(--primary-color)]/5'\n                : 'border-black/5 dark:border-white/8 bg-black/2 dark:bg-white/2',\n            )}>\n              <span className={cn(\n                'shrink-0 text-[9px] font-bold px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full',\n                latestFresh.role === 'ai'\n                  ? 'bg-[var(--primary-color)]/15 text-[var(--primary-color)]'\n                  : 'bg-black/8 dark:bg-white/12 text-gray-500',\n              )}>\n                {latestFresh.role === 'ai' ? 'AI' : '弹幕'}\n              </span>\n              <span className={cn(\n                'flex-1 text-[13px] font-medium leading-snug truncate',\n                latestFresh.role === 'ai' ? 'text-[var(--primary-color)]' : 'text-gray-800 dark:text-gray-100',\n              )}>\n                {latestFresh.text}\n              </span>\n              {/* 底部栏专属大波浪 */}\n              <div className=\"flex items-end gap-[2.5px] shrink-0\" style={{ height: 18 }}>\n                {[0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6].map(i => {\n                  const color = latestFresh.role === 'ai' ? 'var(--primary-color)' : '#6b7280';\n                  return (\n                    <div key={i} className=\"w-[3px] rounded-full\"\n                      style={{\n                        background: color,\n                        height: `${55 + (i % 3) * 20}%`,\n                        animation: `wave-bar ${0.42 + (i % 4) * 0.11}s ease-in-out infinite`,\n                        animationDelay: `${i * 0.07}s`,\n                      }} />\n                  );\n                })}\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          )}\n        </GlassCard>\n      </div>\n    </>\n  );\n}\n\n// ── 工具：从 config 过滤各类 provider ─────────────────────────────────────────\n\nfunction llmList(config: AppConfig | null) {\n  return (config?.AiProviders ?? []).filter(p => (p.ProviderType === 'llm' || !p.ProviderType));\n}\nfunction asrList(config: AppConfig | null) {\n  return (config?.AiProviders ?? []).filter(p => p.ProviderType === 'asr');\n}\nfunction ttsList(config: AppConfig | null) {\n  return (config?.AiProviders ?? []).filter(p => p.ProviderType === 'tts');\n}\n"
  }
}
```

## MODEL ✨

**Refining UI Components** I'm focusing on integrating the new "Voice Interaction Gender" dropdown within the `BotEditModal` in `AI.tsx`, positioning it logically above the `SystemPrompt` textarea. This ensures a clear and intuitive user experience for configuring bot voice characteristics.**Integrating Gender Setting** I'm now investigating the `AiBot` struct in `src/config.rs` to see if it supports a gender field for per-bot configuration. The user's request to relocate the gender selection from a toggle to the settings interface requires this structural consideration, and I'm exploring if the existing `Voice.tsx` implementation needs adjustment.**Tool Command**:

  },
  "id": "read_file_1778511940780_0"
}

config.save()?;\n            return Ok(config);\n        }\n\n        let text = std::fs::read_to_string(CONFIG_PATH)?;\n        Ok(serde_yaml::from_str(&text)?)\n    }\n\n    pub fn save(&self) -> ## MODEL ✨

**Analyzing Z-index Conflicts** I'm currently investigating potential z-index layering issues. It appears the `VoicePicker` component, using `z-50`, might be obscured by the `BotEditModal` in `AI.tsx` (`z-[100]`), especially when the picker is triggered from within a `GlassCard` in the chat area.**Investigating Overlays** I'm re-examining how the `VoicePicker`, with its `z-50` class, is interacting with other elements. The user's description of the "voice selection pop-up being covered by the chat panel" suggests a layering conflict. I'm checking if the `VoicePicker` is indeed rendered within a `GlassCard` that might have `overflow: hidden`, potentially clipping the overlay, despite the `fixed inset-0` positioning.**Tool Command**:

  "response": {

'up-to-date');\n      if (!result) toast.success('已是最新版本');\n    } catch (err) {\n      setUpdateResult('error');\n      toast.error(`检查更新失败: ${err}`);\n    } finally {\n      setChecking(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleInstallUpdate = async () => {\n    setInstallState('downloading');\n    setDownloaded(0);\n    setTotalSize(null);\n\n    unlistenRef.current = await api.onUpdateProgress(({ downloaded: dl, total }) => {\n      setDownloaded(dl);\n      if (total) setTotalSize(total);\n    });\n\n    try {\n      await api.installUpdate();\n      setInstallState('done');\n      toast.success('更新完成，应用即将重启');\n    } catch (err) {\n      const msg = String(err);\n      if (msg === 'already_latest') {\n        toast.info('已是最新版本');\n        setInstallState('idle');\n      } else {\n        setInstallState('error');\n        toast.error(`自动更新失败: ${err}`);\n      }\n    } finally {\n      unlistenRef.current?.();\n      unlistenRef.current = null;\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleOpenConfigDir = async () => {\n    try {\n      await api.openConfigDir();\n    } catch (err) {\n      toast.error(`无法打开目录: ${err}`);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const currentVersion = sysInfo?.version ? `v${sysInfo.version}` : '—';\n  const hasUpdate = updateResult && updateResult !== 'up-to-date' && updateResult !== 'error';\n  const isDownloading = installState === 'downloading';\n  const progressPct = totalSize && totalSize > 0 ? Math.round((downloaded / totalSize) * 100) : null;\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"p-[18px] space-y-4 max-w-3xl\">\n      {/* 版本 */}\n      <GlassCard className=\"p-5\">\n        <h2 className=\"text-[12px] font-semibold mb-4\">版本</h2>\n        <div className=\"space-y-3\">\n          <div className=\"flex items-center gap-4\">\n            <label className=\"w-24 text-[11px] text-gray-500 shrink-0\">当前版本</label>\n            <span className=\"font-mono text-[12px]\">{currentVersion}</span>\n          </div>\n\n          {updateResult === 'up-to-date' && (\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-4\">\n              <label className=\"w-24 text-[11px] text-gray-500 shrink-0\">最新版本</label>\n              <span className=\"font-mono text-[12px]\">{currentVersion}</span>\n              <Chip variant=\"success\" className=\"flex items-center gap-1\">\n                <CheckCircle2 className=\"w-3 h-3\" />已是最新\n              </Chip>\n            </div>\n          )}\n\n          {hasUpdate && (\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-4 flex-wrap\">\n              <label className=\"w-24 text-[11px] text-gray-500 shrink-0\">最新版本</label>\n              <span className=\"font-mono text-[12px] text-[var(--primary-color)]\">{(updateResult as UpdateResult).version}</span>\n              <Chip variant=\"warning\" className=\"flex items-center gap-1\">\n                <AlertCircle className=\"w-3 h-3\" />有新版本\n              </Chip>\n              <button\n                onClick={() => api.openUrl(`https://ghproxy.com/${(updateResult as UpdateResult).link}`)}\n                className=\"flex items-center gap-1 text-[11px] text-[var(--primary-color)] hover:underline\"\n              >\n                <ExternalLink className=\"w-3 h-3\" />镜像下载\n              </button>\n              <button\n                onClick={() => api.openUrl((updateResult as UpdateResult).link)}\n                className=\"flex items-center gap-1 text-[11px] text-gray-500 hover:underline\"\n              >\n                <ExternalLink className=\"w-3 h-3\" />直接下载\n              </button>\n            </div>\n          )}\n\n          {updateResult === 'error' && (\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-4\">\n              <label className=\"w-24 text-[11px] text-gray-500 shrink-0\">检查结果</label>\n              <span className=\"text-[11px] text-red-500\">检查失败，请确认网络连接</span>\n            </div>\n          )}\n\n          {/* 更新日志 */}\n          {hasUpdate && (updateResult as UpdateResult).change_log && (\n            <div className=\"mt-2 rounded-lg bg-black/5 dark:bg-white/5 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/10 p-3\">\n              <p className=\"text-[10px] font-medium text-gray-500 mb-1.5\">更新内容</p>\n              <pre className=\"text-[11px] text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300 whitespace-pre-wrap leading-relaxed font-sans\">\n                {(updateResult as UpdateResult).change_log}\n              </pre>\n            </div>\n          )}\n\n          {/* 下载进度条 */}\n          {(isDownloading || installState === 'installing') && (\n            <div className=\"mt-2 space-y-1.5\">\n              <div className=\"flex items-center justify-between text-[10px] text-gray-500\">\n                <span>{installState === 'installing' ? '安装中...' : `下载中 ${formatBytes(downloaded)}${totalSize ? ` / ${formatBytes(totalSize)}` : ''}`}</span>\n                {progressPct !== null && <span>{progressPct}%</span>}\n              </div>\n              <div className=\"h-1.5 w-full rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-white/10 overflow-hidden\">\n                <div\n                  className=\"h-full rounded-full transition-all duration-300\"\n                  style={{\n                    width: progressPct !== null ? `${progressPct}%` : '100%',\n                    background: 'var(--primary-color)',\n                    animation: progressPct === null ? 'pulse 1.5s ease-in-out infinite' : undefined,\n                  }}\n                />\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          )}\n\n          {installState === 'done' && (\n            <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2 text-[11px] text-green-600 dark:text-green-400\">\n              <CheckCircle2 className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5\" />\n              更新完成，应用即将重启\n            </div>\n          )}\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"flex gap-2 mt-4\">\n          <Button\n            variant=\"primary\"\n            className=\"flex-1\"\n            onClick={handleCheckUpdate}\n            disabled={checking || isDownloading}\n          >\n            <RefreshCw className={`w-3.5 h-3.5 ${checking ? 'animate-spin' : ''}`} />\n            {checking ? '检查中...' : '检查更新'}\n          </Button>\n\n          {hasUpdate && (\n            <Button\n              variant=\"primary\"\n              className=\"flex-1\"\n              onClick={handleInstallUpdate}\n              disabled={isDownloading || installState === 'done'}\n            >\n              <Zap className={`w-3.5 h-3.5 ${isDownloading ? 'animate-pulse' : ''}`} />\n              {isDownloading ? '下载中...' : installState === 'done' ? '已完成' : '自动更新'}\n            </Button>\n          )}\n        </div>\n      </GlassCard>\n\n      {/* 配置 */}\n      <GlassCard className=\"p-5\">\n        <h2 className=\"text-[12px] font-semibold mb-4\">配置</h2>\n        <div className=\"space-y-3\">\n          <div className=\"flex items-center gap-4\">\n            <label className=\"w-24 text-[11px] text-gray-500 shrink-0\">路径</label>\n            <span className=\"font-mono text-[11px]\">{sysInfo?.config_path ?? 'etc/bilidanmaku-api.yaml'}</span>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n        <div className=\"flex gap-3 mt-4\">\n          <div className=\"flex flex-col items-center gap-1\">\n            <IconButton onClick={handleOpenConfigDir} title=\"在 Finder 中打开配置目录\">\n              <FolderOpen className=\"w-4 h-4\" />\n            </IconButton>\n            <span className=\"text-[9px] text-gray-500\">打开目录</span>\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"flex flex-col items-center gap-1\">\n            <IconButton>\n              <Upload className=\"w-4 h-4\" />\n            </IconButton>\n            <span className=\"text-[9px] text-gray-500\">导出</span>\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"flex flex-col items-center gap-1\">\n            <IconButton>\n              <Download className=\"w-4 h-4\" />\n            </IconButton>\n            <span className=\"text-[9px] text-gray-500\">导入</span>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      </GlassCard>\n\n      {/* 数据 */}\n      <GlassCard className=\"p-5\">\n        <h2 className=\"text-[12px] font-semibold mb-4\">数据</h2>\n        <div className=\"space-y-3\">\n          <div className=\"flex items-center gap-4\">\n            <label className=\"w-24 text-[11px] text-gray-500 shrink-0\">DB 路径</label>\n            <span className=\"font-mono text-[11px]\">{sysInfo?.db_path ?? 'db/sqliteDataBase.db'}</span>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n        <div className=\"flex gap-3 mt-4\">\n          <div className=\"flex flex-col items-center gap-1\">\n            <IconButton>\n              <Download className=\"w-4 h-4\" />\n            </IconButton>\n            <span className=\"text-[9px] text-gray-500\">备份</span>\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"flex flex-col items-center gap-1\">\n            <IconButton className=\"bg-yellow-500/20\">\n              <RefreshCw className=\"w-4 h-4 text-yellow-600\" />\n            </IconButton>\n            <span className=\"text-[9px] text-gray-500\">清理</span>\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"flex flex-col items-center gap-1\">\n            <IconButton>\n              <Upload className=\"w-4 h-4\" />\n            </IconButton>\n            <span className=\"text-[9px] text-gray-500\">导出</span>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      </GlassCard>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}
```

}

});\n    return () => unlisten?.();\n  }, [refreshUserInfo]);\n\n  const fetchLoginQr = async () => {\n    setLoadingQr(true);\n    setLoginStatus('pending');\n    try {\n      const data = await api.startLogin();\n      setLoginUrl(data.url);\n      setLoginKey(data.qrcode_key);\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('获取二维码失败:', err);\n    } finally {\n      setLoadingQr(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  // 轮询登录状态\n  useEffect(() => {\n    let timer: NodeJS.Timeout;\n    if (showLoginModal && loginKey && loginStatus !== 'success' && loginStatus !== 'expired') {\n      timer = setInterval(async () => {\n        try {\n          const res = await invoke<any>('poll_login', { key: loginKey });\n          if (res.status === 'Success') {\n            setLoginStatus('success');\n            setShowLoginModal(false);\n            setLoginUrl('');\n            setLoginKey('');\n            if (res.uid) {\n              setUserInfo({\n                uid: res.uid, uname: res.uname, face: res.face,\n                level: res.level ?? 0, vip_status: res.vip_status ?? 0,\n                vip_type: res.vip_type ?? 0, coins: res.coins ?? 0,\n                vip_nickname_color: res.vip_nickname_color ?? '',\n                is_login: true, saved_at: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000)\n              });\n            }\n            setIsLoggedIn(true);\n            setHasConnectedRoom(false);\n          } else if (res.status === 'Expired') {\n            setLoginStatus('expired');\n          }\n        } catch (err) {\n          console.error('Poll login error:', err);\n        }\n      }, 2000);\n    }\n    return () => { if (timer) clearInterval(timer); };\n  }, [showLoginModal, loginKey, loginStatus]);\n\n  const openLoginModal = () => {\n    setShowLoginModal(true);\n    setLoginUrl('');\n    setLoginKey('');\n    setLoginStatus('pending');\n    fetchLoginQr();\n  };\n\n  // 退出登录\n  const handleLogout = useCallback(async () => {\n    await api.logout().catch(() => {});\n    setIsLoggedIn(false);\n    setUserInfo(null);\n    setAutoRoom(null);\n    setHasConnectedRoom(false);\n    window.location.reload();\n  }, []);\n\n  // 未连接时点击交互元素，弹出提示\n  const triggerConnectHint = useCallback(() => {\n    toast.success('请连接房间');\n  }, []);\n\n  // 连接房间成功\n  const handleRoomConnected = useCallback((roomId: string, liveStatus: number, liveTime: string, roomUid?: number) => {\n    const id = parseInt(roomId);\n    setAutoRoom({ roomId, liveStatus, liveTime });\n    setShowRoomModal(false);\n    setHasConnectedRoom(true);\n    // 持久化已连接的房间\n    api.setConnectedRoom(id).catch(() => {});\n    // 拉取主播信息\n    if (roomUid) {\n      api.getAnchorInfo(roomUid).then(setAnchorInfo).catch(() => {});\n    }\n    // 自动启动 WebSocket 监听\n    api.startMonitor(id).catch(() => {});\n  }, []);\n\n  // 断开房间\n  const handleDisconnect = useCallback(() => {\n    setHasConnectedRoom(false);\n    setAnchorInfo(null);\n    api.stopMonitor().catch(() => {});\n    api.setConnectedRoom(null).catch(() => {});\n  }, []);\n\n  if (!loginChecked) return null;\n\n  return (\n    <ThemeProvider>\n      <Toaster\n        position=\"top-center\"\n        richColors\n        duration={1500}\n        closeButton\n        offset={72}\n        toastOptions={{\n          style: { width: 'fit-content', maxWidth: 360, fontSize: 12, padding: '8px 12px', minHeight: 36 },\n        }}\n      />\n      <LoginContext.Provider value={isLoggedIn}>\n      <HashRouter>\n        <div \n          className=\"w-full h-screen overflow-hidden flex relative\" \n          style={{ background: 'var(--background)' }}\n          onContextMenu={(e) => e.preventDefault()}\n        >\n          <BackgroundBlobs />\n          <Sidebar\n            collapsed={sidebarCollapsed}\n            connected={hasConnectedRoom}\n            onToggleThemePanel={() => setThemePanelOpen(!themePanelOpen)}\n            onToggleSidebar={() => setSidebarCollapsed(!sidebarCollapsed)}\n            onToggleSettings={() => setSettingsPanelOpen(!settingsPanelOpen)}\n            onBlockedClick={triggerConnectHint}\n          />\n          <div className=\"flex-1 flex flex-col overflow-hidden  <ChevronRight className=\"w-4 h-4\" />\n                </IconButton>\n              </div>\n            )}\n            <TopBar\n              onToggleNotifications={() => '', info.uid);\n    } catch (err: any) {\n      toast.error(`连接失败: ${err}`);\n    } finally {\n      setLoading(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleMyRoom = () => {\n    if (!userRoom) { toast.error('用户信息未加载'); return; }\n    setRoomId(String(userRoom.room_id));\n    onSuccess(String(userRoom.room_id), userRoom.live_status, userRoom.live_time ?? '', userRoom.uid);\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <>\n      <h2 className=\"text-[15px] font-semibold mb-4\">连接直播间</h2>\n      <div className=\"space-y-4\">\n        <div>\n          <label className=\"text-[11px] text-gray-500 mb-1.5 block\">房间号</label>\n          <div className=\"flex gap-2\">\n            <input\n              value={roomId}\n              onChange={(e) => setRoomId(e.target.value)}\n              placeholder=\"请输入直播间房间号\"\n              className=\"flex-1 h-[34px] px-3 rounded-lg bg-white/60 dark:bg-white/10 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/20 text-[12px] focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-[var(--primary-color)]/50\"\n              onKeyDown={(e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter') handleConnect(); }}\n              autoFocus\n            />\n            <button\n              onClick={handleMyRoom}\n              disabled={!userRoom}\n              className=\"h-[34px] px-3 rounded-lg bg-[var(--primary-color)]/10 border border-[var(--primary-color)]/30 text-[var(--primary-color)] text-[11px] font-medium flex items-center gap-1 hover:bg-[var(--primary-color)]/20 transition-colors disabled:opacity-50\"\n              title=\"连接我的直播间\"\n            >\n              <Home className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5\" />\n              我的房间\n            </button>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n      <div className=\"mt-6\">\n        <Button variant=\"primary\" className=\"w-full\" onClick={handleConnect} disabled={loading || !roomId}>\n          {loading ? '连接中...' : '连接'}\n        </Button>\n      </div>\n    </>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}
```

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    let unl: (() => void) | undefined;\n    api.onSessionSummary(() => {\n      setLatency(p => Math.max(55, ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n  const hasAsrConfig  = asrList(config).length > 0 && !!asrId && asrEnabled;\n  const vadModelOk    = modelStatus?.vad_model_ok ?? false;\n  // ASR 可用条件：有外部 ASR URL（provider 或旧版配置）或本地模型完整\n  const hasAnyAsrUrl  = !!(config?.AsrUrl) || asrList(config).some(p => p.Id === asrId && !!p.APIUrl);\n  const asrModelOk    = hasAnyAsrUrl || (modelStatus?.asr_local_model_ok ?? false);\n  const micEnabled    = hasAsrConfig && vadModelOk && asrModelOk;\n\n  // 麦克风不可用的原因\n  const micBlockReasons: string[] = [];\n  if (!vadModelOk) 服务');\n\n  const handleMicClick = async () => {\n    if (!vadModelOk) {\n      toast.error('缺少 VAD 模型文件，请下载后重试', { description: 'assets/models/silero_vad.onnx' });\n      return;\n    }\n    if
